<time>1596406277431</time><rating>5<//rating>< Text>
Thank you, Offshore Auto Spa!

They did an amazing job on my Black Accord! The paint looks like it's fresh off the assembly line, and virtually free of any swirl marks!

I went with the full exterior service, which includes a wash, wax and detail among many other things, and I'm fully satisfied with how it came out. You will not get a better look with any self-service car wash.

Depending on what service you want, you may spend an hour to a few hours, so I recommend to bringing something for entertainment, or dropping off your vehicle for a little while. 11/10 would recommend to a friend!</Text>

The sweetest girl rang me up and somehow we got to talking about this situation... She not only went over and beyond with her actions and kind words, but also gave me a hug as I was getting misty-eyed.... She showed a true compassion for someone she had only known for two minutes.... I'm an ICU nurse, and as all my mothers issues have unfolded, I've been so busy trying to take care of my family...to have this girl hug me was just what I needed at that time...
I didn't catch her name, but I want to thank her... Thank you for being so kind... Thank you for the essential oils... My mother is SO excited to try them and was very touched by your actions...  We can't thank you enough...

Respectfully,
Mikayla and Terry

<review>I did a lot of research before speaking with any solar suppliers, as the subject was new  to me. Then I contacted four suppliers, two large and two small, and requested a plan and bid to install solar in our 5,750 sq ft home in Rancho Santa Fe. After speaking in detail with each of the four suppliers, Solar Watt was an easy choice.

< UserId.>
107340283471988601604< /UserId.>
< Text>
Im a native to the county, born and raised. I was in high school when this place opened and it was epic. Its pretty much exactly like I remember it. As Walmarts go this location is great; the place is uber-clean and the shelves are stocked with just about everything a human being could want or need and at prices that make being a gluttonous consumer gorging on the sweet teet of our capitalistic society feel all but guilt free.
There is even an actual 'Greeter' that greets you as you enter the store! Its the stuff of department-store-cult-fanatacism! Sure I grew up in the county but in the big city life there is no such thing as Greeters so its always a breath of fresh, country, small town air when I visit the ole Walmart in Martel.
As I've stated, I am a county native so I say this with a warm heart, but any meme you've ever seen about the "people of Walmart" was created and designed with THIS Walmart in mind; THIS IS the archetypal Walmart.
Come for the great prices, vast selection of everything under the sun, or the friendly employees...but above all definitely make the trip as this Walmart offers more than just sustenance for our materialistic desires and compulsions - it offers a portal, a connection to the psyche, our immutable, collective unconsciouses. It presents us with a part of our selves that was long ago; a raw, home-grown slice of culture that is quickly being absorbed by mainstream society. We find humor in the "people of Walmart" because inside of each of us we conceal our own inner "Walmart persona."
This Walmart is truly a transcendent experience.< /Text>
